    int type;

        switch (type) {

            case '+':

                break;

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <ctype.h>

#define MAXOP 100

int main() {
    int type;
    double op2;
    char s[MAXOP];

    while ((type = getop(s)) != EOF) {
        switch (type) {
            case NUMBER:
                push(atof(s));
                break;
            case '+':
                push(pop() + pop());
                break;
            case '*':
                push(pop() * pop());
                break;
            case '-':
                op2 = pop();
                push(pop() - op2);
                break;
            case '/':
                op2 = pop();
                if (op2 != 0.0) {
                    push(pop() / op2);
                } else {
                    printf("error: zero divisor\n");
                }
                break;
            case '\n':
                printf("\t%.8g\n", pop());
                break;
            default:
                printf("error: unknown command %s\n", s);
                break;

void push(double value)
{
  if(top == MAX_SIZE - 1)
  {
    printf("Stack is full\n");
    return;
  }
  
  top++;
  stack[top] = value;
}

void pop()
{
  if(top == -1)
  {
    printf("Stack is empty\n");
    return;
  }
  
  printf("Popped element: %.2f\n", stack[top]);
  top--;
}

void view_head()
{
  if(top == -1)
  {
    printf("Stack is empty\n");
    return;
  }
  
  printf("Head element: %.2f\n", stack[top]);
}

void duplicate()
{
  if(top == -1)
  {
    printf("Stack is empty\n");
    return;
  }
  
  push(stack[top]);
}

void swap()
{
  if(top < 1)
  {
    printf("Not enough elements to swap\n");
    return;
  }
  
  double temp = stack[top];
  stack[top] = stack[top - 1];
  stack[top - 1] = temp;
}

void clear()
{
  top = -1;
  printf("Stack cleared\n");
}

double pop()
{
  if (sp == 0) {
    printf("Stack is empty\n");
    return 0.0;
  } else {
    return stack[--sp];
  }
}
